      <script language="JavaScript" type="text/javascript">
       function make_stars()
{
	var cookies=getCookie('star'),array_cookies,tbody_id,tbody_match,tbody_match_flip,star,star_id;
	$('table tbody').each(function() {
  	tbody_id=$(this).attr('id');
  	if (tbody_id)
  	{
			tbody_match=tbody_id.match(/b(_[0-9]+_[0-9+]+_[0-9]+)/);
			if (tbody_match)
			{
				tbody_match='a'+tbody_match[1];
				star=$(this).find('#'+tbody_match);
				if (!star.length)
				{
					$(this).find('.head2head').first().after('<a id="'+tbody_match+'" title="" class="star" href="#"></a>');
					star=$(this).find('#'+tbody_match);	
				}
				tbody_match_flip=tbody_match.replace(/(a_[0-9]+)(_[0-9]+)(_[0-9]+)/,'$1$3$2');
				if (cookies.match(tbody_match) || cookies.match(tbody_match_flip))
				{
					if (!star.hasClass('isstar')) star.addClass('isstar');
				}
				star.unbind('click').bind('click',function(e)
				{
					e.preventDefault(); 
					var menu=$('#topmenu_full li a.selected').first();
					star_id=$(this).attr('id');
					if ($(this).hasClass('isstar'))
					{
						if (menu.attr('href').match(/t=star/))
						{
							var tr=$(this).closest('tr'),tbody=tr.parent(),tbody_prev=tbody.prev(),tbody_next=tbody.next(),pair,c;
							pair=!tr.hasClass('pair');
							if (tbody.find('.header').length && tbody.next().length && !tbody.next().find('.header').length) tbody.find('tr').not('.header').remove();
							else tbody.remove();
							tbody=tbody_prev.length?tbody_prev.next():tbody_next;
							while(tbody.length)
							{
								c=0;
								tbody.find('tr').each(function()
								{
									if ($(this).hasClass('pair') && pair)
									{
										$(this).addClass('unpair').removeClass('pair');
										c++;
									}
									else if ($(this).hasClass('unpair') && !pair)
									{
										$(this).addClass('pair').removeClass('unpair');
										c++;
									} 
								});
								if (c) pair=!pair;
								tbody_prev=tbody;
								tbody=tbody_prev.next();
							}
							
						}
						else $(this).removeClass('isstar');
						tbody_match_flip=star_id.replace(/(a_[0-9]+)(_[0-9]+)(_[0-9]+)/,'$1$3$2');
						cookies=cookies.replace(new RegExp(star_id,'gi'),'').replace(new RegExp(tbody_match_flip,'gi'),'');
					}
					else
					{
						$(this).addClass('isstar');
						if (cookies.indexOf(star_id)===-1) cookies=cookies+star_id;
					}
					setCookie('star',cookies);
					menu=$('#topmenu_full li a').last();
					menu.html(menu.html().replace(/[0-9]+/,get_favorites(cookies)));
					if (menu.hasClass('selected'))
					{
						if(socket_server!==null)
						{
							socket_server_open=-1;
							socket_server.disconnect();
							var href=menu.attr('href');
							href=href+(href.indexOf('?')==-1?'?':'&')+'u=1';
							last_href='';
							table_update(href,null,null,true); 
						}
					}
					return false;
				});
			}
		}
	});
}

$(document).ready(function() {
	make_stars();
});
      </script>

     <script type="text/javascript">
      var update=15000;
			soundManager.url = 'swf';
            soundManager.onready(function() {
                soundManager.createSound({
                id: 'game',
                url: 'sounds/tennislive_1.mp3'
                });
                soundManager.createSound({
                id: 'score',
                url: 'sounds/sound_3_whistle.mp3'
                });

			});
	$(document).ready(function() { 	var sound_off=checkCookie('sound_off'),sound_on_off=$('#sound_on_off');
	sound_on_off.addClass(sound_off?'on':'off').click(function()
	{
		if (checkCookie('sound_off'))
		{
			deleteCookie('sound_off');
			$(this).removeClass('on').addClass('off');
		}
		else
		{
			setCookie('sound_off');
			$(this).removeClass('off').addClass('on');
		}
	});

	setInterval(function()
	{
		var c=checkCookie('sound_off');
		if(sound_on_off.hasClass('on') && !c) sound_on_off.removeClass('on').addClass('off');
		else if(sound_on_off.hasClass('off') && c) sound_on_off.removeClass('off').addClass('on');
	},3000);
	 });
     </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   //scroll to top
        $(function() {
        var $_goTop = $('#go-top-button');
        $(window).scroll(function(){
            if ($(this).scrollTop() > 60) {
            $_goTop.css({ bottom: '20px' });
            } else {
            $_goTop.css({ bottom: '-100px' });
            }
        });

        $_goTop.on("click", function(){
            $('html, body').animate({scrollTop : 0},700);
            return false;

        });
		});
  </script>

    var s = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0]; s.parentNode.insertBefore(ga, s);
  })();
